e
 Mukesh, Pawan, Akshay and Vinay be hanged? So let us tell you today that at the moment there are five such legal hurdles which are coming between the executions

 har saal magh maheene ke shukla paksh kii saptami tithi ko achala saptami kaa parv manaaya jaataa he
 It is also known by the names Surya Saptami, Rath Arogya Saptami, Suryarath Saptami, Putra Saptami, etc
 yah saptami agar ravivaar ko padati he, to ise bhanu saptami bhi kaha jaataa he
 According to the scriptures, Lord Surya illuminated the whole world with his light on this day, that is why this Saptami is also celebrated as Surya Jayanti
 magh saptami kii mahimavaise to magh kaa puraa maheenaa hi punya maas ke naam se janaa jaataa he
 In this month, Amavasya, full moon and Saptami Tithi of Shukla Paksha are very important
 is saptami ko salbhar kii saptami main sarvshereshth mana gaya he
 Doing this brings good fortune
 magh shukla saptami ko subah niyam ke saath snaan karne se manavaanchit fal miltaa he
 Which should be bathed on this date, facing the east direction, only during the redness of sunrise
 magh shukla saptami main agar prayag main sangam main snaan kiya jaae, to vishesh laabh miltaa he
 On this occasion, by bathing and offering, one attains age, health and wealth
